---
title: "从ES的写入和查询深入了解ES内核"
date: 2022-02-10 11:37:42
categories:
  - es
---

<p></p>
<section style="font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, BlinkMacSystemFont;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px 10px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.6;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px 30px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;line-height:1.6;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-align:center;font-size:14px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;background-color:#407600;color:#ffffff;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:20px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">01</span></strong></span></p>
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-align:center;font-size:14px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">______________________</span></p>
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-align:center;font-size:14px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:16px;color:#407600;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">引言</span></strong></span></p>
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-align:center;font-size:14px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">______________________</span></p>
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">随着数据化时代的到来，海量数据的存储与搜索成了非常关键的一个部分，因为数据承载了应用程序的使用信息，可以用来进行深度挖掘，大数据蕴藏了非常大的价值，除此之外，大数据搜索的实时和准确也成了需要攻克的一环，耗时较长的查询在如今的时代是无法忍受的。</span></p>
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">目前世界上主要的存储框架有两类：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#407600;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">传统的关系型数据库</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">和</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#407600;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">新兴的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">NoSql</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">非关系型数据库</span></span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">（很多人会认为</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">并不是一款数据库，主要还是一款分布式全文检索框架，但是随着</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">功能越来越强大，与数据库的界限也越来越大，这里将其归为</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">NoSql</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的一种）。他们之间的区别是：</span></p>
<ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="margin:0px;padding:0px 0px 0px 2.2em;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;">
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">NoSql</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">查询和写入性能更高：</span></span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">NoSql</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">是基于键值对的，不需要经过</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">SQL</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">层的解析，，同时非关系型数据库比如</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">会有一部分实时数据存在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">os page cache</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">里面，而不是每次数据来都需要写到磁盘，少了很多</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">IO</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">操作，读取也可以从</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">os page cache</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">里面读取，少了很多关系型数据库必须的磁盘操作，所以性能更高。</span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;">
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">NoSql</span></strong></span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;text-decoration:none;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">扩展性更佳</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">：</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">因为基于键值对，数据之间没有耦合性，所以比较容易水平扩展</span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;">
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">关系型数据库查询更友好：</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">使用关系型数据库，比如</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Mysql</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">可以在一个或者多个表之间做非常复杂的数据查询</span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;">
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">关系型数据库数据一致性更强：</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">非关系型数据库一般强调的是数据的最终一致性，但是关系型数据库往往强调的是像</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ACID</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">这样的强一致性。</span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;">
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;text-decoration:none;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">NoSql</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">非关系型数据库更改更灵活：</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">在数据量大的时候，如果想要更新某个表，或者由于业务需求想要为表增加列，是没有办法进行</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">online</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">操作的，比如</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">mysql</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，修改表结构是表级锁，所以修改的时候是会影响其他写入操作的，如果修改失败还需要还原，这时候的耗时更长，而且大数据的表记录也更多，修改表的结构耗时非常长。</span></p>
</li>
</ul><p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">鉴于关系型数据库和非关系型数据库的区别，也就代表了它们分别适用于不同的场景。这里我们将</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Elasticsearch</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">归为</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">NoSQL</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的一员，尽管很多人会将两者分开。</span></p>
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;background-color:#021eaa;color:#ffffff;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">关系型数据库的适用场景：</span></strong></span></p>
<ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="margin:0px;padding:0px 0px 0px 2.2em;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;">
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#021eaa;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">数据量不是特别大的数据</span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;">
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#021eaa;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">对安全性要求高的数据</span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;">
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#021eaa;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">数据格式单一的数据</span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;">
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#021eaa;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">需要进行复杂处理且多表联合处理的数据</span></p>
</li>
</ul><p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;background-color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ffffff;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">非关系型数据库的适用场景：</span></strong></span></p>
<ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="margin:0px;padding:0px 0px 0px 2.2em;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;">
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">海量数据的存储和查询</span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;">
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">多格式的数据存储：文档形式、图片形式等等</span></p>
</li>
</ul><p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">根据关系型数据库和非关系型数据库的优缺点以及各自的适用场景，很容易得出结论：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">非关系型数据更适合处理海量数据的存储和查询</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。</span></p>
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">下面介绍几种主流的非关系型数据库的优缺点以及它们的适用场景：</span></p>
<p style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;background-color:#407600;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ffffff;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">键值(key-value)类非关系型数据库:</span></strong></span></p>
<ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="margin:0px;padding:0px 0px 0px 2.2em;max-width:100%;list-style-type:square;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">for-example: <strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Redis</strong><br style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">典型使用场景：<span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;">内容缓存</span></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">数据模型：<span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">key-value</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;line-height:normal;">键值对，通常底层用</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">hash table</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;line-height:normal;">来实现</span></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">优点：<span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">查找速度快，小而美</span></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">缺点：<span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">对物理内存要求很高：容量收到物理内存的限制，不能用做大海量数据的存储以及高性能读写；在线扩容复杂；不具备自动容错和恢复功能，主机从机的宕机都会导致前端读写请求失败；存储的数据量小于</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">HBase</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">与</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">MongoDB</span></span></p>
</li>
</ul><p style="margin:20px 0px 15px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;background-color:#407600;color:#ffffff;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">列存储</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-family:&#39;mp-quote&#39;, &#39;-apple-system-font&#39;, BlinkMacSystemFont;">类非关系型数据库:</span></span></strong></p>
<ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="margin:0px;padding:0px 0px 0px 2.2em;max-width:100%;list-style-type:square;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<section style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">for-example:<strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">HBase</strong></span></section></li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<section style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">典型使用场景：分布式文件系统。Facebook消息类、淘宝web版阿里旺旺、米聊</span></section></li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<section style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">数据模型：以列簇式存储，将同一列数据存在一起，只有简单的字符串类型</span></section></li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<section style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">优点：查找速度快，可扩展性强，尤其支持海量数据写；适用于简单数据格式写入</span></section></li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<section style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">缺点：不支持SQL语句；数据类型单一：都是字符串类型；不适合于大范围扫描查询</span></section></li>
</ul><p style="margin:20px 0px 15px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;background-color:#407600;color:#ffffff;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">文档型</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-family:&#39;mp-quote&#39;, &#39;-apple-system-font&#39;, BlinkMacSystemFont;">类非关系型数据库:</span></span></p>
<ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="margin:0px;padding:0px 0px 0px 2.2em;max-width:100%;list-style-type:square;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">for-example:</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-family:Palatino;font-size:10px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">MongoDb</span></strong></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">典型使用场景：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">O2O</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">快递应用，将送快递骑手、快递商家的信息（包含位置信息）存储在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">MongoDb</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;">，然后通过</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">MongoDb</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">的地址位置查询，可以很方便地查找附近的商家、骑手等，使得快递骑手能就近接单</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">;</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">游戏场景：存储游戏用户信息；物流场景：存储订单信息；社交场景：存储用户信息；物联网场景：存储智能设备信息</span></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">数据模型：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-family:Palatino;font-size:10px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Key-Value</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;">对应的键值对，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-family:Palatino;font-size:10px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Value</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;">为结构化数据</span></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">优点：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">写数据比较灵活：数据结构要求不严格，表结构可变，不需要像关系型数据库一样需要预先定义表结构；写入延迟低；扩展容易；使用灵活：介于关系型和非关系型之间，类</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">SQL</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">语言，支持二级索引；有</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">MapReduce</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">功能，提供数据分析</span></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">缺点：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">查询性能不高，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">MapReduce</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">性能慢，而且缺乏统一的查询语法；占用空间大；不支持事务操作；无法进行关联操作，不适用于关系多的数据</span></span></p>
</li>
</ul><p style="margin:20px 0px 15px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;color:#575452;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;background-color:#407600;color:#ffffff;letter-spacing:1px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;background-color:#407600;color:#ffffff;letter-spacing:1px;line-height:normal;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">图形</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;background-color:#407600;color:#ffffff;letter-spacing:1px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">(Graph)</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;background-color:#407600;color:#ffffff;letter-spacing:.5px;font-family:&#39;mp-quote&#39;, &#39;-apple-system-font&#39;, BlinkMacSystemFont;">类非关系型数据库:</span></span></p>
<ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="margin:0px;padding:0px 0px 0px 2.2em;max-width:100%;list-style-type:square;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;color:#3e3e3e;font-size:16px;white-space:normal;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">for-example:</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-family:Palatino;font-size:10px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Neo4J</span></strong></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;color:#3e3e3e;font-size:16px;white-space:normal;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">典型使用场景：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">社交网络，推荐系统，公共交通网络，地图等，专注于构建关系图谱</span></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;color:#3e3e3e;font-size:16px;white-space:normal;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">数据模型：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">图结构</span></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;color:#3e3e3e;font-size:16px;white-space:normal;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">优点：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">利用图结构相关算法，比如最短路径寻址，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">N</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">度关系查找等</span></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;color:#3e3e3e;font-size:16px;white-space:normal;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">缺点：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">很多时候需要对整个图做计算才能得出需要的信息，而且这种结构不太好做分布式的集群方案</span></span></p>
</li>
</ul><p style="margin:20px 0px 15px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ffffff;background-color:#407600;letter-spacing:.5px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ffffff;background-color:#407600;letter-spacing:.5px;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ffffff;background-color:#407600;letter-spacing:.5px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">全文检索</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ffffff;background-color:#407600;letter-spacing:.5px;font-family:&#39;mp-quote&#39;, &#39;-apple-system-font&#39;, BlinkMacSystemFont;">类非关系型数据库:</span></span></strong></span></p>
<ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="margin:0px;padding:0px 0px 0px 2.2em;max-width:100%;list-style-type:square;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;color:#3e3e3e;font-size:16px;white-space:normal;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">for-example:</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-family:Palatino;font-size:10px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Elasticsearch</span></strong></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;color:#3e3e3e;font-size:16px;white-space:normal;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">典型使用场景：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;">百度、</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-family:Palatino;font-size:10px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Google</span></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;color:#3e3e3e;font-size:16px;white-space:normal;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">数据模型：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">文档</span></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;color:#3e3e3e;font-size:16px;white-space:normal;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">优点：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">对所有字段都建立索引，查询很快，能满足大多数人的全文检索需求；查询友好</span></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;color:#3e3e3e;font-size:16px;white-space:normal;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">缺点：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">不支持事务；字段类型无法修改；写入性能相对不如</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">HBase</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Redis</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:10px;line-height:normal;">；存储空间占用高</span></span></p>
</li>
</ul></section></section></section></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">针对日志而言，我们的主要目的是实时检索，数据并不会经常更新，也没有事务性操作，所以这里选择了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ElasticSearch</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。鉴于</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ElasticSearch</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的特性，下面会花少量的篇幅介绍它的写入过程，会花大量的篇幅介绍其查询及相关原理。</span></section></section></section></section></section><p></p>
<p style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px 30px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;clear:both;min-height:1em;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:center;font-size:14px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;background-color:#407600;color:#ffffff;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;background-color:#407600;font-size:20px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">02</span></strong></span></p>
<section style="font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, BlinkMacSystemFont;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px 20px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;line-height:.8;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><p style="margin:0px 0px 10px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-align:center;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">______________________</strong></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px 10px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-align:center;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:16px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Helvetica;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的写入过程</span></span></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px 10px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-align:center;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;"><span style="color:#008cb4;font-size:16px;text-align:left;">____________________</span></p>
</section></section></section></section><p></p>
<section style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; text-decoration: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont;"><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;text-indent:30px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;background-color:#407600;color:#ffffff;font-size:15px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;background-color:#407600;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;background-color:#407600;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">写入的大致流程如下：</span></span></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;text-indent:30px;font-family:Palatino;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">1</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">、</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">会先将</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">document</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">发送给</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">coordinate node</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，节点</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">根据</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">document</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">id</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">进行路由</span></span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，将请求转发给指定的节点，一般是</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">primary shard</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">所在的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">node</span></span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">。</span></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;text-indent:30px;font-family:Palatino;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">2</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">、</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">primary node</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">在接收到请求后，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">先将</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">document</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">写入内存</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">buffer</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，然后写入</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">translog</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">。</span></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;text-indent:30px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、如果内存</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">buffer</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">满了或者到了一定的时间（通常是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">1s</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，可以在配置文件中设置，也可以自己通过</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">es</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">restful api</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">进行手动设置），就会将内存</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">buffer</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">数据</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">refresh</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">到一个新的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">segment </strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">文件中，但是此时数据并不是直接写入</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">segment</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">文件，而是</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">先写到</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">os page cache</span></span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">(</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">缓冲</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">IO</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">写</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">中，写到</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">os page cache</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">中之后会清空内存</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">buffer</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">里面的数据。这个过程称为</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">“refresh”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。当数据到了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">os page cache</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">中后，就可以被搜索到了。</span></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;text-indent:30px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">4</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">数据写</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">translog</span></span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，也不是直接写到磁盘里面，同样是先写到</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">os page cache</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">里面，每</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">5s(</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">默认是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">5s</span></span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，可以在配置文件中配置</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">会</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">flush</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">到磁盘里面。所以，极端情况下（主节点和副本节点同时宕机），</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">es</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">是可能存在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">5s</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">中的数据丢失的。</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">translog</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的日志可以在机器宕机之后，帮助数据恢复。当</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">es</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的查询方式是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">GetById</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">时，是直接从</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">translog</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">中获取数据。其他时间是先从</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">os page cache</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">里面获取，再从磁盘里面获取数据。</span></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;text-indent:30px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">5</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">translog</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">文件达到一定大小或者到了一定时间（比如</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">30</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">分钟</span></span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">）之后，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">segment</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">文件会被</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">flush</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">到真正的磁盘空间里面，也就是</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">flush</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">阶段</span></span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。当文件到</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">flush</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">到磁盘之后，索引文件就已经被持久化了，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">translog</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">文件会被清空。</span></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;text-indent:30px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">6</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、当数据</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">写入</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">segment file</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">之后，就建立好了倒排索引</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。</span></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;text-indent:30px;font-family:Palatino;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">7</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">、</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">primary shard</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">在数据成功写入内存</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">buffer</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">translog</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">之后，如果设置了参数：</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">index.write.wait_for_active_shards</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">=1,</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">那么主节点写完后直接返回客户端；如果其值为</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">”all”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，那么必须所有的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">replica nodes</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">都写完以上一系列操作后才返回给客户端。</span></section><p style="margin:0px 0px 10px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;text-indent:30px;line-height:normal;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;">具体流程如下图：</span></p>
</section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;color:#333333;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;,
