!important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">1</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">、</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">将数据写到</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">page cache</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">里面：</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">写入</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">segment</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">文件和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">translog</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">文件时都是先写到</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">os page cache</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">里面，而不是直接</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">flush</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">到</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">segment </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">文件或者</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">translog</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">文件中，减少</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">IO</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">操作，提升写入性能。</span></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">2</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">尽可能顺序写：</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">写到</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">translog</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">文件的时候是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">append</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">到文件中，这里可以尽可能保证刷入硬盘的操作是顺序的。顺序写的速度能达到（</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">600MB/S</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">），而随机读写速度仅为</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">100kb/s</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，顺序读甚至有时候比内存的随机读取还要快。</span></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">以上简单介绍了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">es</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">写入的流程，但是有以下个问题值得深思：</span></section><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="margin:0px;padding:0px 0px 0px 2.2em;max-width:100%;list-style-type:square;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:10px 0px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">es</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的倒排索引具体是怎么实现的，为什么能快速响应搜索请求？</span></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:10px 0px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;font-size:12px;text-indent:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">数据是怎么保证高可用的？</span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:10px 0px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;text-indent:2em;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">数据是怎么保证一致性的？也就是数据写入成功后，再次查询时必须能保证读取到的是最新版本的数据，而不是旧的值？主副本同步的问题是如何解决的？</span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<p style="margin:10px 0px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-indent:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">在同时更新一个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-indent:2em;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">document</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-indent:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的时候，是如何做到多个写入互不影响的</span></span></p>
</li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">
<section style="margin:10px 0px 20px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-indent:2em;font-size:12px;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">写入性能、吞吐量受哪些因素的影响？</span></section></li>
</ul><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;color:#3e3e3e;font-size:16px;background-color:#ffffff;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px 20px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;line-height:.8;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:25px 0px 15px;padding:0px 30px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;white-space:normal;text-align:center;font-size:14px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;background-color:#407600;color:#ffffff;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:20px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">03</span></strong></span></section><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;white-space:normal;color:#3e3e3e;font-size:16px;background-color:#ffffff;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px 20px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;line-height:.8;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><p style="margin:0px 0px 10px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-align:center;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">__________________________</strong></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px 10px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-align:center;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Helvetica;font-size:16px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES倒排索引底层实现原理</strong></span></p>
</section></section></section></section><p style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;white-space:normal;color:#3e3e3e;font-size:16px;background-color:#ffffff;text-align:center;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;">_______________________</span></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px 9px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-align:center;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;font-family:Helvetica;color:#008cb4;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"></p>
</section></section></section></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;text-indent:30px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ElasticSearch</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">最优秀的地方还是在于其强大的检索能力，基于</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">搜索非常快速，还提供了丰富的聚合、排序等以供不同目的的查询。下面将分以下几个部分阐述其查询的底层实现：</span></section><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="margin:0px;padding:0px 0px 0px 2.2em;max-width:100%;color:#3e3e3e;font-size:16px;background-color:#ffffff;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;">
<section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">倒排索引的实现</span></strong></section></li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;">
<section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">聚合查询的实现</span></strong></section></li>
</ul><p style="margin:0px 0px 18px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;text-align:center;line-height:normal;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;background-color:#ff4c00;color:#ffffff;font-size:15px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;background-color:#ff4c00;line-height:normal;font-family:Helvetica;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;background-color:#ff4c00;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">倒排索引的实现</span></span></p>
<section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;font-family:Helvetica;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;letter-spacing:.2px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;">简介</span></span></strong></span></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;text-indent:30px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">简单说的话，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">就是一个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">jar</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">包，里面封装了各种建立倒排索引的算法代码，用</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Java</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">开发的时候，引入</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">lucene jar</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">包，然后基于此去开发就好了。通过</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，可以将已有的数据建立索引，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">会在本地磁盘上，给我们组织索引的数据结构。对于</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">es</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">而言，每个分片都是一个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">索引实例，可以将其视作一个独立的搜索引擎，它可以对</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ElasticSearch</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">集群中的数据子集进行索引并处理相关查询。每个分片又包含多个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">segment</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">（段），每一个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">segment</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">都是一个倒排索引。</span></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;text-indent:30px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">说了这么半天，那究竟什么是倒排索引呢？</span></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.2px;font-size:14px;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">倒排索引简介</span></strong></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;text-indent:30px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">在搜索引擎里面，每个文档都有一个对应的文档</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ID</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">（这个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ID</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">就类似数据库表中的主键来标识一行一样，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">通过</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">DocId</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">来标识一个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Doc</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">），文档内容是一系列关键词的集合。那么倒排索引就是关键词到文档</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ID</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的映射，每个关键词都对应着一系列的文件。这里其实与我们</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">mysql</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">B+ tree</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">索引相反，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">mysql</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">是主键对应关键字，倒排索引是关键字对应主键。索引的本质无外乎是空间换时间，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ElasticSearch</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">对文档中的每个字段都建立了索引。</span></section><section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;font-size:12px;background-color:#ffffff;text-indent:30px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">举个栗子：</span></section><table style="margin:0px 0px <td width="306" height="14" style="margin:0px;padding:4px;border-width:1px;border-style:solid;border-color:#fefefe #7acbf1 #fefefe #000000;max-width:100%;word-wrap:break-word !important;box-sizing:border-box !important;"></td>
