<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">一般而言，如果存储数据是完全不相似的文档，那么正排数据、倒排索引数据、列式数据所需容量占比几乎相同，因为正排数据和倒排数据还会存储唯一字段</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">id</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，所以容量会稍微比列式存储多一些。但是如果文档相似度比较高，那么</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">.tip</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">文件会比较小。一般而言，存储容量是和数据量成正比的，数据的长度和数据量也是成正比的，所以我们在实际应用中可以根据数据量来预估容量。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">有了倒排索引，搜索引擎可以很方便地响应用户的请求。比如之前举的栗子，如果用户输入查询</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Facebook</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，搜索系统查找倒排索引，从中找出包含这个单词的文档</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">id</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">列表，再通过这个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">id</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">列表获取到对应的文档信息。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">了解了倒排索引的概念，下面来看下倒排索引的底层实现。</span></section><p style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:0px 0px 10px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.2px;color:#ab1942;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">倒排索引底层实现</span></strong></p>
<p></p>
<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;font-family:Palatino;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">首先倒排索引由三部分构成：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ff2941;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">单词索引</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">(Term Index)</span></span></strong></span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;">、</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ac39ff;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">单词词典</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">(Term-Dictionary)</span></span></strong></span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;">、</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#0080ff;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">倒排列表</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">(Posting List)</span></span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">单词索引</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">(Term Index)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">：</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">为了更快地找到某个单词，我们为单词词典也建立索引，通过</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term Index</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">可以快速定位到单词在单词词典中的查找位置。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">单词词典</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">(Term Dictionary)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">：</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">搜索引擎的通常索引单位是单词，单词词典是由文档集合中出现过的所有单词构成的字符串集合。单词词典内每一项不仅仅记载单词本身的一些信息，还有一个指向</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">“</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">倒排列表</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的指针。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">倒排列表</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">(Posting List)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">：</span></span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">倒排列表记载了出现过某个单词的所有文档的文档列表及单词在该文档中出现的位置信息及频率。根据倒排列表可知道单词出现在哪些文档里面。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">单词词典的实现是重中之重</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，当单词的数据达到一定规模的时候，其数据格式的设计显得尤为重要。这里我们可以用</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">HashMap</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">来简单描述这个实现结构：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Map&lt;string, list&lt;integer=""&gt;&gt;&lt;/string,&gt;</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，这个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Map</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Key</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">即是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，那它的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Value</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">即是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Postings</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，所以它的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Key</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">集合就是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Dictionary</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">了。在数据量比较小的时候，我们是可以采用数组来实现单词词典，查找的时候使用二分查找，时间复杂度是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">logN</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">；但是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">磁盘的随机读操作是非常昂贵的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">(</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">一次</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">random access</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">大概需要</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">10ms</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的时间</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，所以为了尽可能减少随机读，有必要将一些数据缓存到内存里，但是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">整个单词词典又太大了，无法完整地放到内存里面</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，于是有了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">term index</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">term index</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">就像一本字典的大的章节表，常用的实现方式是通过</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">hash</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">加链表结构和树型结构</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">(b</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">树</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">或者</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">b+</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">树</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。但是随着数据的增加，这样的数据结构占据内存空间还是太大了，后面</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">后面采用了</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">FST</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">BKD</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">树</span></strong></span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">两种数据结构来存储单词词典</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，除此之外，还用到了</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">跳跃表</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">来进行倒排表的合并以及搜索，下面先简单介绍这几种数据结构。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"></section><p></p>
<p style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:20px 0px 15px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;font-size:12px;font-family:Helvetica;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;letter-spacing:.2px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">FST(Finite State Transducer)</span></strong></span></p>
<p style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">比如有这样两个关键字：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Alice</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Alan</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，最后组成一个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">FST</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，就是如下图这样子：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; text-decoration: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont;"></p>
<p></p>
<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">也就相当于你得到了一个有向无环图，有这样一个数据结构，就可以很快查找</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">到某个人名是否存在。</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">FST</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">通过共享前缀来节省空间，内存存放前缀索引，磁盘存放后缀磁块。</span></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Segment</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">上每个字段都有自己的一个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">FST(FSTIndex)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">FST</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">在单个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">（</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">就是单词的意思）的查询上相比</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">hashmap</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">并没有非常明显的优势，甚至可能会慢一些，但是在范围、前缀搜索以及压缩率上有明显的优势，也就是说</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">在内存占用方面优势明显</strong></span></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，其时间复杂度是：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">O(len(str))</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">使用</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">FST</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，最主要的是解决了模糊搜索的问题。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">FST</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">类似字典树，但不是字典树，它由如下特点：</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">1</span><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-style:italic;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;text-decoration:none;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、共享前缀</span></em></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-style:italic;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;text-decoration:none;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">2</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、共享后缀</span></span></em></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-style:italic;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;text-decoration:none;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、确定</span></span></em></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-style:italic;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;text-decoration:none;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">4</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、无环</span></span></em></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:5px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><em style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-style:italic;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;text-decoration:none;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">5</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、接收特定的序列，终止于</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Final</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:none;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">状态，同时会输出一个值</span></span></em></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:20px 0px 15px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;font-size:12px;font-family:Helvetica;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;letter-spacing:.2px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">BKD树(Binary k-dimensional B-tree)</span></strong></span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;font-family:Palatino;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term Dictionary</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">是基于关键字类型是字符串而讨论的，如果关键字类型是数值类，比如浮点数，那么潜在的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">会非常多，所以</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">引入了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">BKDTree</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">BKDTree(Binary k-dimensional B-tree)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">是基于</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">KDTree(k-dimensional B-tree)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，对数据按照维度划分建立一颗二叉树确保树两边节点数目平衡。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;font-family:Palatino;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">KDTree</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">的栗子：</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">BKDTree</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">KDTree</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的变种</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，因为</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">KDTree</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">在有新的节点加入的时候，消耗还是挺大的，类似于</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">LSM</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">merge</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">思路，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">BKDTree</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">也是多个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">KDTree</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，然后持续</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">merge</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">成最终一个。</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">BKDTree</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">内部的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">node</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">必须是一个完全二叉树</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，因为是完全二叉树，所以</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">node</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">不需要存储到它们子</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">node</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的指针</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，直接用乘法就可以了，假如一个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">node</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的位置在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">i</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，那这个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">node</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的左</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">node</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">在位置</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">2i</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，右</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">node</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">2i+1</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。既然叶子节点包含所有点数据，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">node</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">不需要包含它们自己</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的任何数据。</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#99195e;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">更小的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;color:#99195e;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">node</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#99195e;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，意味着更多的数据可以存储在缓存内</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">大量的点数据存储在节点内，也降低了树的深度。</span></strong></span></section><p style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;"></p>
<p style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;"></p>
<p style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; text-decoration: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont;"></p>
<p></p>
<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">更重要的是，</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">BKD</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">树的内部树是不会被修改的</span></span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，这里使用了一个更聪明的方法来添加新的数据：首先，有一个大小为</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">M</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">buffer</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，如果</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">BKD</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">树有</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">N</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">个数据，那么它有</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"> log2(N/M)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">个可修改的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">K-D</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">树。每一个树都是前一个树的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">2</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">倍。数据首先被插入到内存里的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Buffer</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">里，一旦</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Buffer</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">满了，先定位到第</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">1</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">个为空的树。这个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Buffer</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的数据，以及空树之前所有节点的数据一起生成一个满的平衡树。其读写性能和空间利用率都非常优秀。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:20px 0px 15px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;font-size:12px;font-family:Helvetica;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;letter-spacing:.2px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Skip-List跳跃表</span></strong></span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">利用</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Skip-List</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">来实现倒排链的合并和docId的查找。如下图，跳跃之间有一个固定的间隔，这个需要建立跳跃表的时候就指定好，下图中的间隔是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">SkipList</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的层次有三层。</span></section><p></p>
<p style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; text-decoration: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont;"></p>
<p></p>
<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">再举个例子，如下图，我们要合并两个链表：</span></section><p></p>
<p style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; text-decoration: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont;"></p>
<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">假设已经合并到</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">8</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">了，现在我们继续移动两个表的指针，第一个表移到</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">16</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">处，而第二个表移到</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">41</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">处，两者中较小项为</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">16</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，这时候我们并不继续移动上面的指针，而是检查跳表指针的目标项，第一个表指针的目标项为</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">28</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，仍然比</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">41</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">小，这个时候就直接跳过了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">19</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">23</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，合并的时候就可以不用比较</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">19</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">23</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，节省了时间。而且，如果某个链很短，会大幅减少比对次数。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">熟悉了以上三种</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">中用到的数据结构，下面我们来看下</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">是如何应用这些数据结构来进行底层实现的。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:20px 0px !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong Index的实现</span></strong></span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">在介绍之前，我们首先来看看</span><span 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont;"></p>
<p></p>
<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term Index</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">仅仅只是存储</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">通过它可以快速定位某个特定的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">term dictionary</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">中的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">offset</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，然后根据</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">offset</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">往后顺序查找来找到对应的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。所以</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term Index</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">不需要存储所有的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，仅仅只是一些前缀与</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">block</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">指针，再通过一定的压缩手段可以使整个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term Index</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">缓存到内存中</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。从</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term Index</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">查到对应的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term Dictionary</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">block</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">位置之后，再去磁盘上找</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ff2941;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">大大减少了磁盘随机读的次数</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;font-family:Palatino;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term Dictionary</span><span !important;">.tim</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，格式如下：</span></section><p style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; text-decoration: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont;"></p>
<p></p>
<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;font-family:Palatino;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term Index</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">就是图中的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">.tip</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">部分，它由一个或者多个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Segment</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">上每个字段都有自己的一个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">FST(FSTIndex)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">记录在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">.tip</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">上，图中</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">tip</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">里有</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">M</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">FSTIndex</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，代表该</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">上拥有</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">M</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">个字段。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;font-family:Palatino;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">.tim</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">文件中的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">分块是按照</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">.tip</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">文件中的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">FST</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">来的</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Block0</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">中所有的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">都是以</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">”abd”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">为前缀的，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Block1</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">中所有的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">都是以</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">“abe”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">为前缀的。每一个</span><span Header</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，里面知名这个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Block</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">包含几个</span><span !important;">N</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Suffix</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">里面包含了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">N</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">个后缀，比如</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Block0</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">中包含</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;">”i”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">“j”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">。</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Stats</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">里面包含了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">N</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">个统计信息，每个统计信息包含</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">docFreq</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">和</span><span !important;">Metadata</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">里面包含了指向倒排表文件</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span !important;">Block</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">是数组，准确的说，就是把一系列的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Block</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">序列化写到文件上</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;font-family:Palatino;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span !important;">.tim</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">的结合就类似于一种</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;">Trie</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">中的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Block)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Trie</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">的一个变种，它主要是将后缀进行了压缩，降低了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Trie</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">的高度，从而获取更好的查询性能。</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">采用了其思想，将一个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">的查询分成两部分，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">里面的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Block</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">是数组。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">1</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、快速试错：在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Dictionary</span><span !important;">MIN</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">的意思是当某个状态节点的子节点个数超过</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;">MAX</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">的意思是当个数超过</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box abdf abdg abdh abei abej abek abel abem aben</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">。所形成的状态树如图所示，根据</span><span Dictionary</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">就可以比</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px
