<p></p>
<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;font-size:12px;font-family:Helvetica;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;letter-spacing:.2px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Postings(</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;">倒排表</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;letter-spacing:.2px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;">实现</span></span></strong></span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;font-family:Palatino;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Postings</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">采用了两种关键的编码格式：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;color:#ff2941;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">PackedBlock</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ff2941;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">VIntBlock</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">。</span></section><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:0px;padding:0px 0px 0px 2.2em;max-width:100%;color:#333333;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, BlinkMacSystemFont;"><li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;">
<section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">VIntBlock</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">用来存储复合数据类型：</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">既能存储变长整型也能存储字符串。</span></section></li>
<li style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;">
<section style="margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">PackedBlock</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">用来存储单一整数数组结构：</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">只能存储固定长度的数组，它的压缩方式是将每个元素截断为一个预算的长度以达到压缩的目的。</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">PackeBlock</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">相当于实现了向量优化，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">通常会将整个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">PackedBlock</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">加载到内存，既可以减少</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">IO</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">操作数，又能提高解码的性能，比较适合存储少量的数据。</span></section></li>
</ul><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">采用以上两种数据结构的目的都是为了方便数据压缩。之所以两种数据混用是因为采用</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Menlo;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">PackedBlock</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">带来了向量优化，更加节省空间，但因为其只能存储定长数组，所以两者结合对空间的占用率更高。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Posting</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">被拆成三个文件：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">.doc</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">文件，基本所有查询都会用到，一般的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Query</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">用到</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">.doc</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">也就够了；</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">.pox</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，近似查询会需要用到；</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">.pay</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，主要用于</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">payloads</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">搜索。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">.doc</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">文件：</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">该文件是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Posting</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的必要文件</span></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，其他两个文件是可以通过配置省略的。</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">.doc</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">文件上存储的信息如下：</span></section><p style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; text-decoration: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont;"></p>
<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;font-family:Palatino;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">每个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">上都有成对的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">TermFreq</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">SkipData</span></strong><span !important;">SkipData</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">是为</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">TermFreq</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">构建的跳表结构，所以它们是成对出现的，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#407600;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">SkipData</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">的主要作用是在根据</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">DocId</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">获取</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">时可通过</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">SkipData</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">快速跳转</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">。</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">TermFreq</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">存储了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Posting</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">上最核心的内容，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">DocID</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">TermFreq</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，分别表示文档号和对应的词频</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">。</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">TermFreq</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;">采用的是混合存储，由</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">PackedBlock</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">VIntBlocks</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;">两种结构组成</span></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">。</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">PackedBlock</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">是定长的，默认是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">128</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Integers</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，所以在不满</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">128</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">个值的时候，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">采用</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">VIntBlocks</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">结构存储。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">预先编译了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">64</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">PackedFormat</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">编码器和解码器，即针对</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Long</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">以内的每种长度的数据都有自己的解码器和编码器，以提高解码的性能。</span></span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;font-family:Palatino;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">.doc</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">文件中，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">TermsFreq</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">的格式如下：</span></section><p style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; text-decoration: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont;"></p>
<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;font-family:Palatino;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">PackedBlock</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">由</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">PackedDocDeltaBlock</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">PackedFreqBlock</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">组成，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">PackedDocDeltaBlock</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">主要是存储</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">对应的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">DocId</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">列表，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">PackedFreqBlock</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">存储</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">DocId</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">中的词频信息。之所以用到</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">PackedBlock</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">这一数据结构是为了将数据的长度统一化从而达到压缩的目的，因为</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">预先变异了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">64</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">PackedFormat</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">编码器和解码器，即针对</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Long</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">以内的每种长度的数据都有自己的解码和编码器，以提到编解码的性能。用</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">VIntBlock</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">来存储复合数据类型也是为了通过变长整型编码以达到压缩的目的。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">.doc</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">文件中还有一个重要元素</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">SkipData</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">SkipData</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">是为</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">TermFreqs</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">构建的跳表结构，主要是搜索时的优化，主要是减少集合间取交集时需要比较的次数</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，比如在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Query</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">被粉刺起分成多个关键词时，搜索结果需要同时满足这些关键词的，此时需要将每个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">对应的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">DocId</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">集合进行析取操作，通过跳表能够有效减少比较的次数。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">三大组成元素的内部实现就介绍到这儿了，下面我们再来看一下</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Elasticsearch</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">是如何做到上亿量级的聚合查询的？</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:25px 0px 15px;padding:0px 30px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:center;font-size:14px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;background-color:#407600;color:#ffffff;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:20px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">04</span></strong></span></section><section style="font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, BlinkMacSystemFont;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section
