!important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">_____________________________</strong></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px 10px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-align:center;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Helvetica;font-size:16px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES聚合查询</strong></span></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px 10px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-align:center;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;"><span style="font-size:16px;text-align:left;color:#000000;">_________________________</span></p>
</section></section></section></section><p></p>
<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Elasticsearch</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">对于大数据量（上亿量级）的聚合是如何实现的，首先我们看这样一个栗子：比如我们要统计索引中排名前三的国家及人口数量，按照</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Elasticsearch</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的分布式原理，会在每个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">shard</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">中求出前</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，然后再汇总节点根据每个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">shard</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的返回再汇总求</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">top3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，这个时间问题来了，如下图：</span></section><p style="font-style: normal; font-weight: normal; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px; text-decoration: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont;"></p>
<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">汇总节点拿到的数据是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">shard1/shard2/shard3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">返回的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">A B C E</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">四个国家做最终汇总，但是很明显，国家</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">D</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">其实可以排入前三，如果按照以上方面会导致结果不准确，如何解决呢？有如下几个方法：</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">1</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、每个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">shard</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">返回更多的结果，每个节点返回</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">top100</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，减少误差。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;font-family:Palatino;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">2</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">、将相同的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">发送到同一个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">shard</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">，比如</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">A</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">国都在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">shard1</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">（</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">route</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">方法）。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、最暴力的方法，直接不分片，一个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">shard</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">以上三个方法都有明显的缺点：</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">方法一：到底需要返回多少冗余数据不得而知，而且返回冗余数据的计算代价也非常昂贵。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">方法二：如果</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">term</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">有成千上万甚至上亿，每一个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">index</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">TB</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">级别的呢，这个时候每个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">shard</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">会巨大，并且还需要业务感知，需要在入库的时候指定</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">route</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">方法三：单个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">shard</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的容量是有限的，大小一般建议是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">30GB-50GB</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，并且单个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">shard</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">无法体会分布式的魅力。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">这里可以介绍下</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Hadoop</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Map-Reduce</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">是怎么做的</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。每个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">map</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">任务产生了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">1/2/3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">三份数据（这个三份数据可以有很多理解，比如表面上的三个国家，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">hash</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">之后的三个取模值，甚至三个区间等等），这里有一个很特别的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">shuffle</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">过程，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">shuffler</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">过程会把每一个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">map</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的同一份数据送到一个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">reduce</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">里面，对于这个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">reduce</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">来说，对这一份数据进行统计就能够得到这一份数据的精确结果。其他的数据也类似，这样整个过程就能够得到精确值。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">没有这样做，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">并不把没有处理过的文档数据直接通过</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">route</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">发送到指定的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">shard</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，而是通过</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ad1603;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">打分机制</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">来得到相对准确的值。</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Elasticsearch</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">具体的解决思路是：</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">1</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、首先根据打分标准从每个分片查询，并进行排名，取前</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">数据，发给</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">coordinate node</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">；</span></strong></span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#888888;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">2</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">coordinate node</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">在收到所有分片的数据之后，再进行汇总查询并排名，取前</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">数据，然后根据这</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">条数据的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">id</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，到不同的分片获取数据。</span></strong></span></section><p></p>
<p style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;font-size:12px;font-family:Helvetica;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;letter-spacing:.2px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">打分机制</span></strong></span></p>
<p></p>
<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">什么是打分？<strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">确定文档和查询有多么相关的过程被称为打分</strong>，打分模型有很多种，常用的是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">TF-IDF</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">BM25</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">TF-IDF</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">属于向量空间模型，而</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">BM25</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">属于概率模型</span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，但他们的评分公式差别并不大，都使用</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">IDF</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">方法和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">TF</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">方法的某种乘积来定义单个词项的权重，然后把和查询匹配的词项的权重相加作为整篇文档的分数，后续在查询的时候会根据这个分数进行排名。下面简单介绍一下</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">TF-IDF</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">BM25</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">两种打分模型，以此来理解</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Elasticsearch</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">查询的过程。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Menlo;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">TF(Term Frequency</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">：词频</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Menlo;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">：即单词在该文档中出现的次数，词频越高，相关度越高；</span></strong></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Menlo;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">IDF(Inverse Document Frequency</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">：逆向文档频率</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Menlo;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">)</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">：与文档频率相反，简单理解为</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Menlo;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">1/DF</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。即单词出现的文档数越少，相关度越高。</span></strong></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">假如</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">索引中，有三篇文档，词条</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">“ICU”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的文档频率是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">2</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，因为它出现在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">2</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">篇文档中，文档的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">IDF</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">源自得分乘以</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">1/DF</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">DF</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">是该词条的文档频率，也就说，由于</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ICU</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">词条拥有更高的文档频率，其逆向文档频率值会降低。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">词条</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">“the”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的文档频率是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，它在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">篇文档中都出现了，注意：尽管</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">the</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">在后两篇文档中都出现了两次，但是它的词频还是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，因为，逆文档词频只检查词条是否出现在某篇文档中，而不检查它在这篇文档中出现了多少次，那是词频该干的事儿。</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">IDF</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">是一个非常重要的因素，比如我们搜索</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">”the 996 ICU”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，单词</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">”the”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">几乎出现在所有文档中，如果这个东东不被均衡一下，那么</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">“the”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的频率将完全淹没</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">996</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。所以，逆文档词频就有效的均衡了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">“the”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">这个常见词的相关性影响。以达到实际的相关性得分将会对查询的词条有一个更准确地描述。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;font-family:Palatino;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">BM25</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">是一种基于概率的打分框架，比如可以配置某个</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">field</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">”similarity”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">来设置，也可以通过配置全局的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">index.similarity.default.type</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">来配置。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">除此之外，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">boosting</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">也可以用来修改文档的相关性从而改变文档的得分从而影响排名。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">运用打分机制是为了让结果相对来说更加准确，但是如何使亿级查询更快呢？</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;font-size:12px;font-family:Helvetica;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;letter-spacing:2px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;letter-spacing:.2px;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">fieldcache</span></strong></span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene4</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">之前需要把结果全部拿到再读取原文进行排序，这种方式显而易见占用内存空间大而且效率很低，为了加速</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">实现了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">fieldcache</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">把读过的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">field</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">放进内存中</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。新版本的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">引入了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">DocValues</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">DocValues</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">是一个基于</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">docid</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的列式存储，通过</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">docid</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">可以快速读取到该</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Doc</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的特定字段的值。当我们拿到一系列的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">docid</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">后，用堆排序进行排序就可以使用这个列式存储，当然这个列式存储会占用额外的空间。一般用于</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">sort</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">agg</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">等需要高频读取</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">doc</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">字段值的场景。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">但是把读过的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">fielddata</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">放进内存里面，这个行为是</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">“</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">延迟加载</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，也就是在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">fielddata</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">第一次被查询的时候加载到内存，那有可能在首次加载遇到停顿数秒卡顿没有反应的情况，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">想了一个方法：预加载，也就是随着新分段（刷新、写入和合并等方式）的创建，启动字段预加载可以使那些对搜索不可见的分段里面的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">fielddata</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">提前加载。这就意味着首次命中该新分段的查询不需要触发</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">fielddata</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的加载，因为已经加载到内存了。</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ad1603;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">预加载只是简单地将载入</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Menlo;color:#ad1603;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">fielddata</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ad1603;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的代价转移到了索引刷新的时候，而不是查询的时候，大大提高了搜索体验。</span></section><p></p>
<p style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;font-size:12px;font-family:Helvetica;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;letter-spacing:2px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;letter-spacing:.2px;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Global Oridinals</span></strong></span></p>
<p></p>
<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">但是把</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">fielddata</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">放到内存仍然是一笔不小的开销，有什么方法可以降低其内存使用吗？</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;color:#000000;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">还真想了一种方法：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:15px;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:15px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">全局序号</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:15px;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">(Global Ordinals)</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#000000;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。简单来说，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">全局序号就是用数值存储代替字符串存储，以节省内存加载</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Menlo;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">fielddata</strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">时的数据大小。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">假设我们有十亿文档，每个文档都有自己的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">status</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">状态字段，状态总共有三种：</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">status_pending</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">status_published</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">status_deleted</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。如果我们为每个文档都保留其状态的完整字符串形式，那么每个文档就需要使用</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"> 14 </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">到</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"> 16 </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">字节，或总共</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"> 15 GB</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">。但是我们可以对这三个字符串用整型数字编号，序号字符串在序号列表中只存储一次，每个文档只要使用数值编号的序号来替代它原始的值。这样可以将内存使用从</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"> 15 GB </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">降到</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"> 1 GB </span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">以下！</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">全局序号分布在索引的所有段中，是存在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">doc values</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">之中的，但是它和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">fielddata</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">加载一样，默认也是延迟构建的，首个访问索引内</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">fielddata</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的请求会触发全局序号的构建，这也会带来一定的延迟，这里，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">也有办法，就是通过<strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">预构建全局序号使得其加载到内存发生在新分段对于搜索可见之前</strong>。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;font-size:12px;font-family:Helvetica;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;letter-spacing:2px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;letter-spacing:.2px;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">索引预热器</span></strong></span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">除了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">“</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">预加载</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">“</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">全局序号</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">还有一个东东：索引预热器，即允许我们指定一个查询和聚合必须要在新分片对于搜索可见之前执行，也就是通过预先填充或预热缓存让用户永远无法感知到延迟的风波，也就是将冷缓存的代价转移到了刷新的时候。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">预热器的目的就是注册那些可以代表用户产生流量压力的查询，从而将合适的内容载入缓存。</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">当新建一个分段时，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ElasticSearch</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">将会执行注册在预热器中的查询。执行这些查询会强制加载缓存，只有在所有预热器执行完，这个分段才会对搜索可见。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;text-decoration:underline;color:#ff4c41;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">索引预热器的缺点是会增加新分段对于搜索可见的时间。</span></strong></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:25px 0px 15px;padding:0px 30px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:center;font-size:14px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;background-color:#407600;color:#ffffff;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:20px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">04</span></strong></span></section><section style="font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, BlinkMacSystemFont;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><section style="margin:0px;padding:0px 20px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;line-height:.8;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><p style="margin:0px 0px 10px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-align:center;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;"><span style="color:#000000;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">____________________________</strong></span></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px 10px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-align:center;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Helvetica;font-size:16px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;color:#000000;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ES<span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;text-align:center;line-height:normal;">在</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-family:Helvetica;font-size:14px;text-align:center;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;text-align:center;line-height:normal;">之上的封装</span></strong></span></p>
<p style="margin:0px 0px 10px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;text-align:center;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;"><span style="color:#000000;font-size:16px;text-align:left;">_________________________</span></p>
</section></section></section></section><p></p>
<section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Elasticsearch</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">底层的搜索和索引创建是基于</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">来实现的。为什么不直接用</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">来存数据读数据呢？原因如下：</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">1</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">数据不可靠：</span></span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">生成的</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">segment</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">是放在内存里面的，机器如果宕机或者断电，数据会丢失；</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">2</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">不支持部分更新：</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">不支持文档的部分更新，只支持创建和删除，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">部分更新</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">”</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">这一强需求无法保证；</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、</span><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#ab1942;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">不能保证高可用：</span></span></strong><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">是单机的，不是分布式，无法保证高可用。</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;font-family:Palatino;color:#000000;line-height:2em;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">而</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ElasticSearch</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">改善了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;">以上三个方面的缺点：</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">1</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;color:#407600;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">translog</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">机制：</span></strong></span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">数据同时写</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">segment</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">和</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">translog</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">文件，即使宕机，我们也可以通过</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">translog</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">来进行数据恢复；</span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">2</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#407600;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#407600;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">通过删除</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#407600;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">+</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#407600;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">替换索引的方式支持部分更新，通过乐观锁</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#407600;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">+</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#407600;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">版本控制来保证部分更新中数据同步问题；</span></strong></span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">3</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">、</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;color:#407600;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;"><strong style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">通过分片和副本机制老达到高性能和高可用</strong></span></section><section style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:15px 0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;"><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">可以说，</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">ElasticSearch</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">利用了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的优势，弥补了</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;line-height:normal;font-family:Palatino;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">Lucene</span><span style="margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;box-sizing:border-box !important;word-wrap:break-word !important;">的不足。其查询优势和在分布式方面的增强与扩展使得它的应用也越来越广泛。</span></section><p></p>
<p style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;color:#333333;font-family:&#39;-apple-system&#39;, BlinkMacSystemFont;"></p>
<p style="font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;text-transform:none;white-space:normal;word-spacing:0px;text-decoration:none;margin:0px;padding:0px;max-width:100%;clear:both;min-height:1em;letter-spacing:.5440000295639038px;text-align:justify;text-indent:30px;font-size:12px;line-height:normal;"></p>
